if ('consoleLog' in window &&
'generic' in window &&
'ad_utils' in window &&
'custom' in window &&
'monitoring' in generic &&
'document_is_ready' in generic) {
try{
inside.call(this);
}catch(e) {
if ( window.ueLogError ) {
if(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined'){
e.message = failureMessage;
}

e.logLevel = "ERROR";
ueLogError(e);
}

(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined') ){
console.error(failureMessage);
}
}
} else {
if( (document.location.hash.match('debug=1')) &&
(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined') ){
console.error(failureMessage);
}
}
};

    <script async>
        function getAdsForSlotsCall() {
            if (window && window.ad_utils && window.ad_utils.makeAtfSlotsCall) {
                window.ad_utils.makeAtfSlotsCall(true,
                    'https://www.boxofficemojo.com/_json/getads/bom_other?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.imdb.com%2Fother%2F&subPageType=maindetails&adLayout=bom_desktop_other&targeting=c%3D1&isMobile=false',
                    'inline20,inline40,sis_pixel',
                    {"inline20":{"767":"320x50","9999":"970x250","1279":"970x250","1023":"728x90"}});
            }
        }

        var debounce = function(func, wait, immediate) {
            var timeout;
            return function() {
                var context = this, args = arguments;
                var later = function() {
                    timeout = null;
                    if (!immediate) func.apply(context, args);
                };
                var callNow = immediate && !timeout;
                clearTimeout(timeout);
                timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
                if (callNow) func.apply(context, args);
            };
        };

        window.addEventListener("resize", debounce(getAdsForSlotsCall, 750));
        getAdsForSlotsCall();
    </script>

    <p class="mojo-gutter a-text-italic">Holiday Season 2017 is November 3-January 4, 2018.</p><style>
